---
id: adaptiveapi
title: Adaptive API
---

Adaptive API solution will help to simplify integration of DIEP platform with third party APIs. Standard input is converted to API specific input and the response from the API is converted to standard output. 

## Components of Adaptive API

>![ADAPTIVEAPI_HL](../../static/img/docs/diep2/Adaptive-API-HL.jpg)

Different Components of Adaptive API solution are explained below – 

### APIM I

Azure API management module is responsible for calling transformation api using the input key and forwarding the output to the APIM E (External) endpoint. Upon receiving response from APIM E, it will do the output transformation by calling the transformation api again with the output key mentioned. The output of this transformation is sent back to the client. 

### Transform

This is an API which is responsible for actual transformation. 
>![ADAPTIVEAPI_HL](../../static/img/docs/diep2/Transformation-Flow.png)

Transformation type can be any of the following. 

- **JQ** – For Simple transformation
- **JSONATA** – For slightly complex transformation
- **JavaScript** – For complex transformation which can’t be achieved using JQ or JSONATA 

Transform API takes the following parameters as a POST request -

- **key** – Key to identify config which is stored on BLOB storage. This will be used by the API for transformation. 
- **data** – Data which needs to be transformed

Sample request


In the header, we need to pass the **Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key**. 

The output of this api is a JSON which contains the following - 

- **settings** - This is settings json file based on which the transformation happens and downloaded by the API from blob storage using the key which is specified in the input request.

- **data** - Actual transformed data. 

Sample response
```jsx

{
    "settings": {
        "transformationType": "JSONATA",
        "transformationExpression": "( $print:= null; $companyId:= \"R0104\"; $productId:= \"HO17\"; $marketId:= \"M0003\"; $coverageId:= \"HO\"; $coverageDesc:= \"Homeowners\"; $SicID:= \"HOME\"; $CSRId:= \"cogitate\"; $getFeesAndTaxesAmount:= function($code) { $getFeesAndTaxesExist($code) = false ? 0 : $getFeesAndTaxesExist($code).Amount }; $getFeesAndTaxesRate:= function($code) { $getFeesAndTaxesExist($code) = false ? 0 : $getFeesAndTaxesExist($code).Value }; $getTaxes:= function() { $c:= { \"Tax1Code\": \"SLT\", \"Tax1Name\": \"SurplusLine Tax\", \"Tax1Rate\": $getFeesAndTaxesRate(\"PRETAX\"), \"Tax1Amount\": $getFeesAndTaxesAmount(\"PRETAX\"), \"Tax2Code\": \"SOF\", \"Tax2Name\": \"Stamping Fee\", \"Tax2Rate\": $getFeesAndTaxesRate(\"STF\"), \"Tax2Amount\": $getFeesAndTaxesAmount(\"STF\"), \"Tax3Code\": \"NA\", \"Tax3Name\": \" \", \"Tax3Rate\": 0, \"Tax3Amount\": 0, \"Tax4Code\": \"NA\", \"Tax4Name\": \" \", \"Tax4Rate\": 0, \"Tax4Amount\": 0, \"Tax5Code\": \"NA\", \"Tax5Name\": \" \", \"Tax5Rate\": 0, \"Tax5Amount\": 0, \"Tax6Code\": \"NA\", \"Tax6Name\": \" \", \"Tax6Rate\": 0, \"Tax6Amount\": 0, \"Tax7Code\": \"NA\", \"Tax7Name\": \" \", \"Tax7Rate\": 0, \"Tax7Amount\": 0, \"Tax8Code\": \"NA\", \"Tax8Name\": \" \", \"Tax8Rate\": 0, \"Tax8Amount\": 0 } }; ```
```

Important part of the transform API is the settings file which is downloaded from Azure blob storage based on the key which is specified in the request. It has the following attributes

- **transformationType** - Specifies the type of transformation which needs to be applied. Accepted values are JSONATA, JQ and JS. 
- **transformationExpression** - Either transformationExpression or file needs to be mentioned. If transformation expression is big then creating a file and uploading to blob storage is a better option. This contains the actual transformation expression. 
- **key** - Unique name to identify the file.
- **description** - Optional parameter. Description of the transformation. 
- **forwardingUrl** - Mandatory for input transformation. Not required for ouput transformation. The URL for the APIM E endpoint. 
- **file** - Name of file which contains the actual transformation expression. Not mandatory if transformationexpression is specified. 

Sample settings file
```jsx
{
        "transformationType": "JSONATA",
        "transformationExpression": "( $print:= null; $companyId:= \"R0104\"; $productId:= \"HO17\"; $marketId:= \"M0003\"; $coverageId:= \"HO\"; $coverageDesc:= \"Homeowners\"; $SicID:= \"HOME\"; $CSRId:= \"cogitate\"; $grossCommision:= 22.5; $invoiceStatusList:= [3, 9, 7, 15, 20]; $invoicingStates:= [\"CT\",\"MA\",\"MD\",\"ME\",\"NH\",\"NJ\",\"NY\",\"OH\",\"PA\",\"RI\",\"VT\"]; $taxedFeeStates:= [\"GA\", \"NC\", \"SC\", \"VA\"]; ```
```


### APIM E

This end point is invoked from APIM I endpoint and is responsible for calling the external API. This will pass the required authentication to invoke the external API successfully. Once the response is received back from the API it is sent back to APIM I to do the output transformation.

### LCNC

Using LCNC users will be able to enter the required settings and expression for transformation. 


## Integration using Adaptive API

Steps to Integrate an API using Adaptive API

### Setting up APIM Endpoint which calls the external api

Login to Azure portal. Open API Management. Select the environment specific APIM for Adaptive API. 
>![APIM_SETUP](../../static/img/docs/diep2/Select_Adaptive_API.png)

Click on APIs.
>![APIM_SETUP](../../static/img/docs/diep2/APIs.png)

Click on Add API.
>![APIM_SETUP](../../static/img/docs/diep2/Add_NEW.png)

Fill Details
>![APIM_SETUP](../../static/img/docs/diep2/Fill_API.png)

Click on Add Operations
>![APIM_SETUP](../../static/img/docs/diep2/Add_Operation.png)

Fill details for Operations
>![APIM_SETUP](../../static/img/docs/diep2/Operation_Fill.png)

Click on Policy
>![APIM_SETUP](../../static/img/docs/diep2/Click_Policy.png)

Add Policies to call the external API
>![APIM_SETUP](../../static/img/docs/diep2/Add_Policy.png)

Test the setup
>![APIM_SETUP](../../static/img/docs/diep2/Tes.png)

### Create Transformation expression

This will require 2 transformation expression. One for input transformation and other for output transformation. For input transformation, the expression should transform input data to expected output which will be consumed by third party api. The output transformation should work with response of the external api and it should convert it to a structure which your application will understand. To create transformation expression you can use below links - 

- https://try.jsonata.org/
- https://jqplay.org/

### Create Config File

2 configuration files need to be created. One for input transformation and other for output transformation. Setting file should be in this format.

Sample settings file
```jsx

        "transformationType": "JSONATA",
```

### Upload Config File

The Configs created in above step should be uploaded to environment specific blob storage containers created for Adaptive API. 

### Test the setup

To test, pass the input key and output key to environment specific adaptive api apim url. 

### Sample Request

**Type**: POST

**URL**: https://adaptiveapiapm.azure-api.net/api/invoke?inputkey=uwvazz4neeeho3.r1t&outputkey=uwvazz4a.r1t

**Header**: 
Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key:< -- Key -->
